Having ZERO experience with weight lifting, I was fearful of further injury, but intrigued by their emphasis on functional movement. At our first meeting, Nate listened to my concerns and said he could help. He set me up with Mee for foundations. Mee is awesome! She paid close attention to ensure I had the techniques down and was so careful about injury prevention. That is the great thing about BSCF!  The coaches take an interest in each athlete, providing encouragement and emphasizing technique for an effective, injury free workout.   After 6 months, I feel great and have learned a lot (and not just from googling all those abbreviations!). üòä  I look forward to the WODs and the camaraderie and support I get from the staff and whole community is just gravy. Thanks Mee, Nate, Lindsay, Kristin, Cindy and the rest of the BSCF staff. Oh, and it‚Äôs not a gym, it‚Äôs a box.</review>

<Review>Transfer from Mavericks gym.... First squat max attempt in 4 months. 335# squat PR for #beachsidecroasfit today.. 4 months ago when I started crossfit, I began very hesitant and very skeptical. First off, bench press is never programmed in the workouts, my favorite (you can still do them though on your own free time there). And I had the fear that all my strength gains made on my own would disappear since we hardly ever do max days... Not only did I hit a new PR, but I'm in way better shape than I've ever been! The programming is the best, and although it's not geared towards mirror muscles if you're worried, you get so much more out of crossfit, as Nathan will remind you your fitness is a marathon, not a sprint. Your body will gain incredible mobility and you'll be able to move around more efficiently and in less pain. Most importantly, and the thing you can't find at a normal gym, is the community. Friends at the gym, lifting buddies, faces you recognize at your normal gym who *might*
cheer on your heavy lifting attempts, aren't community. Here at beachside, you will make friends with those doing the same as you and suffering through a workout with you, and you will look forward to seeing those same faces every workout. Here at Beachside, they'll all always cheer you on and push you to do better, every lift, every PR attempt, every tail end of a terrible cardio workout. It takes a little blind trust to walk away from something you've been so use to, something you're so comfortable with in being at your normal gym. Don't be ok being comfortable, challenge yourself, and do it here, at a place with coaches that will help you, and a community that will push you to the best fitness you've ever had.<//Review>< pics>

<rating>2< /rating>< review>
On Sunday evening it was a very relaxed setting. It started off with stale chips with a different tasting salsa that upset my wife's stomach. My daughter said the enchilada and beans were cold with clumps of unmelted cheese. The food has always been pretty good. The enchilada and taco with rice and beans was not hot. The plate was warm but not hot. I was very disappointed. The rice was very bland. The cheese in the beans clumped up because it was not hot at 140 degrees. The service was ok but I did not want to complain there. It would have been uncomfortable in that tight nit atmosphere. Improvement needed. The place is getting complacent and taking the food for granted.< /review>

<UserId.>108036868540787493107</UserId.>< review>
After giving this place a few tries I can definitely say that I do not like their food.  The pupusas are small and thin with very little filling, the beans are watery, the Salvadorian cream is watered down and runny, (you literally need a spoon to eat the beans, lol).  You would expect that these foods are suppose to be the staples and highlights for a Salvadorian restaurant and they are not. The flavors are not bad and do taste authentic, however the textures are gross.  It seems as though they are trying to save money by watering down and skimping on their foods.  Which is why I will no longer eat here...<//review>

My first time and I think it is one of the best salvadorean places I've eaten at. Very authentic! And the prices are a plus. $6.99 for the breakfast plate which includes refried blended black beans, sour cream, fried plantain, avocado, fresh white soft cheese, scrambled eggs with tomato and onions, includes handmade tortilla or french roll. You got to try this place. My mom had the chicken soup with veggies she loved it. We also purchase tamales for $1. Its just amazing. Cash only place! But it's worth it.< /review>

Daaaayummmm good BBQ! It's that simple. It was old school, proper smoked n settled BBQ. When the smoker is on the trailer of an 18-wheeler, you know something big is happening. Definitely in the top 10 of my global BBQ hunting. Seasoned just right, smoke ring just deep enough, just tender enough, and still moist enough. I've been dying to try Horn BBQ for months and let me tell you it exceeded all expectations! The brisket was unbelievably juicy and tender, the ribs were mind blowing and even the turkey (which I usually don't love at BBQ places) was moist and flavorful. The sides were also a huge hit , especially the mac n' cheese, coleslaw, and potato salad. I am DEFINITELY going back for more brisket, and to try out their beef ribs and sausage.

Their service is also top notch. I ordered a hefty amount for a team picnic and the Horn crew (shout out to Melissa!)were incredibly helpful with the whole process, even calling me to answer all of my questions and help coordinate my order. I haven't tried waiting in line yet - although it's totally worthy of a wait - but the online ordering process was super easy, just make sure you do it a few days in advance to guarantee you get everything your heart desires.< /Review>

This is my second time visiting Horn BBQ. The first visit was last year before the holiday season kicked off. I waited in line for almost 1 hour and 30 minutes. That is way too long to stand outside in the cold to order food. I ordered the brisket, 2 sausage links, ribs, pulled pork and baked beans.  That was a little over $100.

February's 2021 visit I was pleasantly surprised by a short line. Ordered ribs, pulled pork and 1 sausage link. The casing for the sausage was a bit tough but flavorful. The ribs were very moist and tender as well as the pulled pork. A new addition was the sliced bread given with each order. It was either previously toasted or just hard. Overall I would visit again but I can't stand in a long line.  This visit was a little over $75.< /text>

Horn BBQ is definitely some of the best bbq ive ever had, especially in the bay area....but...the wait (2.25hrs on a Saturday) was something I couldn‚Äôt justify in the experience, some of the food was cold by the time i was able to order which i felt could of took it to the next level but overall the BBQ craving was satisfied.

4< /rate>
< Text>
Waited about 3 hours total after arriving an hour before opening. We tried everything except the pit beans.

Beef ribs were by far the best thing we had there - tender, juicy, and flavorful...mouthwatering overall.

Pork ribs, pulled pork, and turkey were also fairly tender, juicy, and tasty.

Brisket was unfortunately kind of dry and not melt in your mouth as we were expecting/hoping for.

Sausage links had a good flavor but also kind of dry.

The sides were all good - collards weren't too salty, slaw refreshing, mac & cheese and Granny's potoates nice and cheesy, and potato salad very satisfying.

The banana pudding was surprisingly good and not too sweet.

We thought it was worth the wait as a first time try. Hopefully, there will be more days open with shorter waits eventually.<//Text>

<user>104144734762969944656<//user><GmapID>0x80857f104a587995:0xfbe5612e5aea9103<//GmapID>< review>
I really, really want to give this place five stars. I have to share the fact that TL;DR, if you pre-order your brisket its about $50/lb because the whole brisket at $250 is only 4.8-4.9 lbs. If you stand in line to order in person on Fri/Sat/Sun its only $30/lb. I do not understand the price difference and was not able to get an explanation. $50/lb for pre-order seems wrong because I'm actually buying in bulk ... so I'm being punished for buying in advance?

The only reason I know what the prices are is because I actually had a chance to get Horn BBQ before my pre-order once. A friend stopped by, and showed me the menu, and I got some brisket at $30/lb. Having been to many places in Texas, New York, SC, SD, etc. and all along the west coast, I have to say their brisket is far superior and actually comparable to Texas vs. any other place I've had in California or the west coast.

However, I do feel that it changes my mind when its $30/lb which is still expensive but worth it, to $50/lb.

I was so excited to pre-order and I couldn't believe how small it was. I understand if this was disclosed up front, but why would the price for public sale be different from pre-order?!

At $50/lb, this is the most expensive brisket or meal I've ever had in terms of quantity & type of meat. While it was good, it was not $50/lb good. I think it would have been 5 stars if the price was consistent especially for those who spent lots of money to support this business. I'm disappointed and hope they will change this in the future. For now, it is not likely I'll go back to try again.</review>

< Review>
The bicycle was badly beaten up with a bent gooseneck and untrue wheels. They fixed up my bicycle for an affordable price and the bike had much improved speed and handling, with the feeling of a brand new bike. The place is welcoming, with it's upbeat office aesthetic and a staff of people ready to assist you, and give you all of the options to ensuring your ride, is a ride of your choice. When compared to other places in Lakewood, such as Performance Bicycle Shop, this place is your best option. I highly recommend you give this place a visit when you are in the area for a bicycle that can be tuned to not only your liking, but to your desire.</Review>
